      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/3515.Ann_Marie_MacDonald">About Ann-Marie MacDonald</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/3515.Ann_Marie_MacDonald"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1253837223p3/3515.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/3515.Ann_Marie_MacDonald">Ann-Marie MacDonald
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
861
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14699951975034489047">Ann-Marie MacDonald is a Canadian playwright, novelist, actor and broadcast journalist who lives in Toronto, Ontario. The daughter of a member of Canada's military, she was born at an air force base near Baden-Baden, West Germany.<br/><br/>MacDonald won the Commonwealth Writers Prize for her first novel, Fall on Your Knees, which was also named to Oprah Winfrey's Book Club.<br/><br/>She received the Governor General'</span>
  <span id="freeText14699951975034489047" style="display:none">Ann-Marie MacDonald is a Canadian playwright, novelist, actor and broadcast journalist who lives in Toronto, Ontario. The daughter of a member of Canada's military, she was born at an air force base near Baden-Baden, West Germany.<br /><br />MacDonald won the Commonwealth Writers Prize for her first novel, Fall on Your Knees, which was also named to Oprah Winfrey's Book Club.<br /><br />She received the Governor General's Award for Literary Merit, the Floyd S. Chalmers Canadian Play Award and the Canadian Author's Association Award for her play, Goodnight Desdemona (Good Morning Juliet).<br /><br />She also appeared in the films I've Heard the Mermaids Singing and Better Than Chocolate, among others.<br /><br />Her 2003 novel, The Way the Crow Flies, was partly inspired by the Steven Truscott case.<br /><br />She also hosted the CBC Documentary series Life and Times from 1996 to 2007.<br /><br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/AnnMarieMacDonaldAuthor">https://www.facebook.com/AnnMarieMacD...</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="14699951975034489047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/2547473-the-way-the-crow-flies">Quotes from The Way the Crow ...</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;There are some stories you can't hear enough. They are the same every time you hear them. But you are not. That's one reliable way of understanding time.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/70844-there-are-some-stories-you-can-t-hear-enough-they-are">46 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Afterwards, in bed with a book, the spell of television feels remote compared to the journey into the page. To be in a book. To slip into the crease where two pages meet, to live in the place where your eyes alight upon the words to ignite a world of smoke and peril, colour and serene delight. That is a journey no one can end with the change of a channel. Enduring magic.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/497017-afterwards-in-bed-with-a-book-the-spell-of-television">23 likes</a>
